		Kamborapasu Dombo Chinkura Nechisake Nechagadzike Mambo Rupanadamananga Gumboremvura Toloa Matuzvianye
		Mukombwe Nyamhandu Basvi Tohwechipi Nyatsimba Ngwato Molwa Tamasiga Seogola Mucombo Inhamunda Ningomoxa
		Chiraramuro Chombo Peranhe Chicanga Nyacuimbiri Samutumbu Mupunzagutu Gowera Nyarumwe
	}
	female_names = {
		Behati Achieng Nuru
	}
}

mosan_culture_group = {
	graphical_culture = northamericagfx

	#Note the Mosan division, one of Sapir's, is conclusively disproven as far as I'm concerned. Nevertheless, it is a valid and feasible idea to put all these troublesome little one-culture-per-group
	#cultures into a single group and call it Mosan. Is extremely attractive from a gameplay and continuity point of view, and you can't exactly say they were completely disimilar, sharing the same
	#Sprachbund, habits, a bio region. Conversely, how much did the Waskashans really share with the Inuit, or even Alutiq, possible very distant linguistic ties aside? And do we really want
	#Haida all by itself or shoved in with the Athabaskan supergroup? I can't imagine anyone would take issue with this, unless it is to suggest adding Salishan to this group. That said, This a world
	#class cultural variety hotspot, so I'm going with Basque-like one-culture-per-group cultures here, at least for now. Old Mosan idea repurposed into a Haida group, because internal code shenanigans =p.

	haida = { #Language isolate. Formerly placed with Athabaskan, but this is accepted to be a mistake. Attempts have been made to place it with most other groups to limited success
		primary = HDA
		dynasty_names = {
			Kiusta Kung Yan Hiellan Skidegate "Cha'atl" Haina Kaisun Cumshewa Skedans Tanu Ninstints
			Masset Atewaas Jaahguhl Kayung "Hlk'yah GaawGa" Klinkwan Sukkwan Howkan Kasaan
		}
		male_names = {
			"Nanni Chaddi" "Na tio tish" Sitahle Oahtekah Ahzaah Kootzzah Moketaveto Ohtoahnesotowheo Harkkahome
			Munamenek Otoahnisto Mahvipah Choseta Nahtan Konzhontaco Bazheech Tillaka Chacon Dasoda-hae Cochise Juh
			Delshay Goyaale
		}
		female_names = {
			Dahteste Ilthgozay Gouyen Lozen Tohayea
		}
	}
}
